UI/VideoOptionsInstructions=玩遊戲或觀賞戰鬥錄影時，你可以按 CTRL-F11 來開啟或關閉遊戲影像錄製。影像將以 Theora OGV 的格式儲存於你的使用者目錄下《星海爭霸II》的影像資料夾中。錄製高品質的影像可能會嚴重減緩遊戲執行速度。 /// You can toggle in-game video recording by pressing CTRL-F11 while playing a game or watching a replay. Videos are stored in your user directory's StarCraft II Videos folder in Theora OGV format. Recording high quality video may considerably slow down your game experience.
UI/VideoOptionsTooltips/AudioQuality=<c val="ffffff">音頻品質：</c><n/>提高音頻品質可提供更好的音頻保真度，但會產生較大的影像檔。 /// <c val="ffffff">Audio Quality:</c><n/>Increasing audio quality will provide greater audio fidelity at a cost of larger video files.
UI/VideoOptionsTooltips/FrameRate=<c val="ffffff">幀率：</c><n/>幀率指的是每秒錄製的畫面數。較高的幀率可讓影像播放過程更加流暢，但會產生較大的影像檔。在較高的幀率下錄製影像可能會減緩遊戲執行速度。 /// <c val="ffffff">Framerate:</c><n/>Framerate refers to the number of frames recorded per second. A higher framerate will result in smoother video playback at a cost of larger video files. Recording at a higher framerate may slow down your game experience.
UI/VideoOptionsTooltips/RecordAudioCheckbox=<c val="ffffff">開啟音頻：</c><n/>開啟影像的錄音功能。 /// <c val="ffffff">Enable Audio:</c><n/>Enables recording audio with your video.
UI/VideoOptionsTooltips/RecordTriggers=<c val="ffffff">觸發器錄製：</c><n/>開啟此選項可以透過遊戲中的觸發器來錄製影片。玩家可用「MovieStartRecording」觸發器編輯地圖以便錄製影片。如果你不希望在某些地圖上自動錄製影像，請關閉此選項。 /// <c val="ffffff">Record From Triggers:</c><n/>Enabling this option will allow you to record video from in-game triggers. Players can create maps with "MovieStartRecording" triggers to facilitate the creation of movies. Keep this option off if you do not want videos to automatically record on certain maps.
UI/VideoOptionsTooltips/Resolution=<c val="ffffff">解析度：</c><n/>決定錄製影像的像素多寡。較高的解析度會有較好的畫面品質，但是錄製速度較慢。為求最佳效果，請使用符合你遊戲畫面比例的解析度。 /// <c val="ffffff">Resolution:</c><n/>Determines the size in pixels of the recorded video. Higher resolutions have much better image quality, but they are slower to record. For best results, use a resolution that matches your game's aspect ratio.
UI/VideoOptionsTooltips/SlowGame=<c val="ffffff">錄製影像時，放慢遊戲速度：</c><n/>決定是否在錄製影像時，放慢遊戲速度以彌補效能的降低。這樣可以提高錄像品質，但無法在多人對戰模式下使用。關閉此選項設定會降低幀率進而影響錄像品質，但不會影響所錄製的音效。 /// <c val="ffffff">Slow Game while Recording:</c><n/>Determines whether or not game time will slow down to adjust for the performance drop while recording video. This will result in better looking videos, but it cannot be used while participating in multiplayer games. Videos recorded with this option disabled will record the drop in framerate, but your audio will be unaffected.
UI/VideoOptionsTooltips/VideoQuality=<c val="ffffff">影像品質：</c><n/>決定錄製影像所使用的壓縮比例。較高的影像品質將有較高的畫面品質，但會產生較大的影像檔。 /// <c val="ffffff">Video Quality:</c><n/>Determines the amount of compression used when recording your video. Greater video quality will result in better image quality but much larger video files.

Keep this lower if breathing and other incidental sounds are triggering voice chat.
